## p. 7 (#21) ###############################################

The Summer Social Register, issued late in June, with Dilatacines
in July, is limited to the country or foreign addresses received
since the November winter issues, from the prominent families of
New York, Washington, Philadelphia, Chicago, Boston, St. Louis,
Pittsburgh, Baltimore, Buffalo and Southern Cities combined in
one volume.
Families not appearing in this summer issue may be found at
the addresses given in preceding issues,
The winter issues for each city will appear in November, with
Dinteres in December, January, February and April. They will
record the full names and addresses of members of prominent
families, grouped together, the clubs to which they belong, and
the marriage, death and European arrival and departure of
each person as it may occur.
Misses 12
to 17
The names of Juniors
Mors 14 to 20
under the
appear
names of older members of their families.
The subscription is $5.00 per annum for each city.
A subscription of $20.00 will include all the issues for
New York, Washington, Philadelphia, Chicago, Boston, St.
Louis, Pittsburgh, Baltimore, Buffalo and Southern Cities from
Richmond to Atlanta.
Information for November should be received before
October 15.
FOREIGN POSTAGE.
Complaints have been received from families and bankers of short
postage upon invitations and other bulky correspondence.
Foreign postage is limited to half the weight of domestic letters,
and if only five cents be a fixed to a letter weighing more than one-
half ounce, not only the extra postage, but an additional fine of five
cents, is charged to the receiver.
